6665: Port. udp - Reserved. tcp - IRCU.
6666: Port. udp - Reserved. tcp - IRCU.
6667: Port. udp - Reserved. tcp - IRCU.
6668: Port. udp - Reserved. tcp - IRCU.
6669: Port. udp - Reserved. tcp - IRCU.
tcp: Transmission Control Protocol. If a port is open, the operating system completes the TCP three-way handshake, and the port scanner immediately closes the connection to avoid performing a Denial-of-service attack.[3] Otherwise an error code is returned. This scan mode has the advantage that the user does not require special privileges. However, using the OS network functions prevents low-level control, so this scan type is less common. This method is "noisy", particularly if it is a "portsweep": the services can log the sender IP address and Intrusion detection systems can raise an alarm. (Source - https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Port_scanner#Types)
